# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
a circle is a curve where all the points have the same distance r from a point called center ^qX2ulSbk

equation of circle with center a and b and 
radius r ^tRjqEOac

the derivative is simply the instantaneous rate of change of the equation, if the 
curve grows the first derivetive is positive, if it shrink negative and if it stays
the same 0 ^R2zq5lfE

the marginal cost is the rate of
change of the total cost ^eu6IxdGt

it states that the signed area is the sum on infinitely small squares represented by
a hight of the instantaneous rate of change ^zsLA5VWa

you can sum or sub matrices of the same size by simply summing or subtracting the terms
in the same postions ^amAA4Pgb

it is the matrix for which if you multiply the matrix you have you get the
identity matrix out, it is noted as A^-1 ^JxSHFe2Q

identical left side, so no solutions
or infinite solutions ^fdhOUhFl

if deteminant not 0 the matrix is invertible and the equations
have 1 solution ^n5AQJQ0S
